                            <div class="row question">
                                <div class="col-md-12" style="padding-left:0px; padding-right:0px;">
                                    <div class="row">
                                        <div class="serial">
                                            <span>Question 71 </span>
                                        </div>
                                        <div class="questionText" style="display: block;">
                                            <p>একটি বল 4 kg ভরের স্থির বস্তুর উপর ক্রিয়া করায় বস্তুটি 6 সেকেন্ডে <span class="math-tex"><span class="MathJax_Preview" style="color: inherit; display: none;"></span><span class="MathJax" id="MathJax-Element-96-Frame" tabindex="0" style="position: relative;" data-mathml="<math xmlns=&quot;http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML&quot;><mn>30</mn><mtext>&amp;#xA0;</mtext><mi mathvariant=&quot;normal&quot;>m</mi><msup><mi mathvariant=&quot;normal&quot;>s</mi><mrow class=&quot;MJX-TeXAtom-ORD&quot;><mo>&amp;#x2212;</mo><mn>1</mn></mrow></msup></math>" role="presentation"><nobr aria-hidden="true"><span class="math" id="MathJax-Span-1012" style="width: 4.249em; display: inline-block;"><span style="display: inline-block; position: relative; width: 3.467em; height: 0px; font-size: 122%;"><span style="position: absolute; clip: rect(1.306em, 1003.47em, 2.386em, -999.998em); top: -2.234em; left: 0em;"><span class="mrow" id="MathJax-Span-1013"><span class="mn" id="MathJax-Span-1014" style="font-family: MathJax_Main;">30</span><span class="mtext" id="MathJax-Span-1015" style="font-family: MathJax_Main;">&nbsp;</span><span class="mi" id="MathJax-Span-1016" style="font-family: MathJax_Main;">m</span><span class="msubsup" id="MathJax-Span-1017"><span style="display: inline-block;                                         <div class="serial">
                                            <span>Question 76 </span>
                                        </div>
                                        <div class="questionText" style="display: block;">
                                            <p>Which one of the following is the correct Negative form of the sentence? “Every mother loves her child”.</p>

                                        </div>
                                    </div>
                                </div>
                                <div class="row questionOptions">
                                    <div class="col-sm-12 row questionOption">
                                        <div class="input-group" style="align-items: center;">
                                            <div class="input-group-prepend">
                                                <span class="input-group-text">A</span>
                                            </div>
                                            <div class="input-group-append questionTable">
                                                <label style="margin-left:5px;"><p>Every mother does not love her child.</p>
</label>
                                                
                                            </div>
                                        </div>
                                    </div>
                                    <div class="col-sm-12 row questionOption">
                                        <div class="input-group" style="align-items: center;">
                                            <div class="input-group-prepend">
                                                <span class="input-group-text">B</span>
                                            </div>
                                            <div class="input-group-append questionTable">
                                                <label style="margin-left:5px;"><p>There is no mother who does not hate her child.</p>
</label>
                                                
                                            </div>
                                        </div>
                                    </div>
                                    <div class="col-sm-12 row questionOption">
                                        <div class="input-group" style="align-items: center;">
                                            <div class="input-group-prepend">
                                                <span class="input-group-text">C</span>
                                            </div>
                                            <div class="input-group-append questionTable">
                                                <label style="margin-left:5px;"><p>Every mother hates her child.</p>
</label>
                                                
                                            </div>
                                        </div>
                                    </div>
                                    <div class="col-sm-12 row questionOption">
                                        <div class="input-group" style="align-items: center;">
                                            <div class="input-group-prepend">
                                                <span class="input-group-text" style="font-weight:bold;">D</span>
                                            </div>
                                            <div class="input-group-append questionTable">
                                                <label style="margin-left:5px;"><p>There is no mother but loves her child.</p>
</label>
                                                <span class="fas fa-check"></span>
                                            </div>
                                        </div>
                                    </div>
                                </div>
                                    <div class="row solveText" style="display: block; padding:10px; color:#077307; overflow-x: auto; background-color: #d7f7d4;">
                                        <span style="color: black !important; font-weight: bold;">Solution:</span>
                                        <br>
                                        <span style="color: black !important;"><p>Sentence এ Every থাকলে negative করার ক্ষেত্রে 'none but' ব্যবহৃত হয়।</p>
</span>
                                    </div>

</label>

</label>

                                                <span class="input-group-text">C</span>
                                            </div>

                                                <label style="margin-left:5px;"><p>Interesting</p>
</label>
                                                <span class="fas fa-check"></span>

                                        <br>
                                        <span style="color: black !important;"><p>Dull অর্থ নিস্তেজ এবং Interesting অর্থ আকর্ষণপূর্ণ। তাই এরা antonymous.&nbsp;</p>
